GEOTECHNICAL ENGINEERING OBSERVATIONS
SOIL NAIL INSTALLATION AND TESTING
HONOAPIILANI HIGHWAY SHORELINE IMPROVEMENTS AT LAUNIUPOKO
ISLAND OF MAUI HAWAII
Dear Mr Fujiwara
This letter report summarizes our geotechnical engineering observation services
performed during the soil nail installation and testing for the Honoapiilani Highway
Shoreline Improvements at Launiupoko project located on the Island of Maui Hawaii
In general this letter report presents our field observations and the results of testing
performed for the soil nails from through August 10 2013
PROJECT CONSIDERATIONS
This project involves emergency road repair due to erosion damage to the existing
shoreline along Honoapiilani Highway Route 30 between Launiupoko Point and
Puamana Beach Park as a result of the ocean waves on the Island of Maui Hawaii The
existing concrete barriers on the shoreline side of the roadway were displaced and
undermining of the concrete barrier structures was noted This project was to install a new
pavement wall to support the road The project location and general vicinity are shown on
the Project Location Map Plate 1
Two soil nailed retaining wall structures designated as Walls A and B were installed
on the ocean side of the highway Walls A and B are about 240 and 560 linear feet
respectively Corrosion resistant stainless steel bars were specified for the nails In
addition a revetment consisting of 1 ½ to 2 ½ ton stones nominal diameter 3 feet was
utilized in front of the soil nailed walls The bottom of the soil nail walls was at about
Elevation 2 Mean Sea Level MSL for Wall A and about Elevation 5 and 2 feet MSL
for Wall B To facilitate construction Wall B was modified The bottom of the soil nail wall
for Wall B was raised from Elevation 2 to 5 MSL between Station to
214 21
KSF Inc
Page 2
W O 6694 10
GEOLABS INC
Hawaii California
A total of 63 8 inch diameter soil nails with nail length of 10 feet were specified for
Wall A For Wall B a total of 318 8 inch diameter soil nails with nail length of 17 feet were
specified The soil nail was composed of No 9 Type 2205 Stainless Steel bar and
4 000 psi cement grout Verification and proof testing were specified for the soil nails
SOIL NAIL INSTALLATION AND TESTING
Soil Nail Installation
Verification and production soil nail installation was performed by AIS Construction
A total of 4 pre production soil nails three for Wall A and one for Wall B were installed for
the project In addition a total of 63 and 228 soil nails were installed for Walls A and B
respectively Wall B was modified with a higher bottom of wall elevation Therefore a
total of 92 original soil nails were deleted The soil nails were installed using a Kaiser
Spyder 4x4 Cross drill rig The Spyder drill rig was equipped with a downhole hammer
and an 8 inch diameter drill bit The approximate locations of the pre production and
production soil nails are shown on the Soil Nail Identification Plans Plates 2 1 through 2 5
The installation of the verification soil nails Nail Nos TA TA1 TA2 and TB was
performed on and July 12 and 17 2013 for Walls B and A respectively
The production soil nails for Wall A Nos A1 through A63 were installed between July 23
2013 and August 10 2013 The production soil nails for Wall B Nos B1 through B212
and B303 through B318 were installed between and
The verification soil nails for Wall A were drilled to lengths of about 10 feet Nail
Nos TA and TA1 and about 17 feet Nail No TA2 at an inclination about 15 degrees
from the horizontal For Wall B the verification soil nail was drilled to a length of 15 feet at
an inclination about 15 degrees The length of the production soil nails for both walls
ranged from about 17 to 19 feet After the hole was drilled to the specified length the hole
was cleaned by blowing out the cuttings and loose material in the drill hole A 1 25 inch
diameter Grade 75 galvanized and epoxy coated bar was installed in the drilled hole for
the verification soil nails For the production soil nails a 1 125 inch diameter Type 2205
Stainless Steel bar was installed Temporary steel casing about 8 inch diameter was
also installed into the drilled hole Centralizers were placed along the soil nail at 2 foot
from the ends and at 5 foot intervals
A ½ inch diameter PVC grouting tube was installed along the reinforcing bar for
grouting purposes Grouting began progressively from the bottom to top through the
grouting tube until fresh grout appeared at the top of the hole The grouting tube was
removed after the completion of the grouting operation A summary of the soil nail
installation is provided in the Summary of Soil Nail Installation and Testing Plates 3 1
through 3 15 The soil nail installation records are provided in Appendix A
Soil Nail Testing
In accordance with the project plans performance testing was performed on a
verification soil nail at Walls A and B Since the verification soil nail Nail No TA for
KSF Inc
Page 3
W O 6694 10
GEOLABS INC
Hawaii California
Wall A failed prior to reaching the maximum test load additional verification soil nails were
installed Nail Nos TA1 and TA2 Based on the performance tests performed for Wall A
the production soil nails for Wall A were lengthened to 17 feet In addition to the verification
testing a minimum of five percent of the production soil nails were proof tested
Production soil nails
and B316 were proof tested
In general the verification soil nails were loaded to maximum performance test
loads of about 50 and 60 kips for Walls A and B respectively The production soil nails
were loaded to maximum proof test loads of about 27 and 45 kips for Walls A and B
respectively The nail head movements for the soil nails at each load increment up to the
maximum test load were measured and recorded The results of the soil nail testing are
provided in the Summary of Soil Nail Installation and Testing Plates 3 1 through 3 15
The soil nail test results are provided in Appendix B
LIMITATIONS
It should be noted that it is not possible to continuously observe all activities
occurring simultaneously on a construction site therefore some of the work for the soil
nail installation and testing may have occurred without our direct observation
Our services were performed in accordance with generally accepted standards of
geotechnical engineering practice no warranty is expressed or implied Provision of
construction monitoring by an engineer is not insurance nor does it guarantee
construction of any type The contractor shall retain responsibility for the quality of their
work for adhering to the contract documents and for repairing defects regardless of when
they are found

CLOSURE
We appreciate the opportunity to provide geotechnical engineering services to
KSF Inc and the State of Hawaii Department of Transportation Highways Division on
this project If you have questions or need additional information please contact our
office
Respectfully submitted

A 1 2 inch dia PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level
Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
Total of 6 bags of 94 lb cement were used to grout the borehole

Meyco FIX Flowcable was added to mix grout about 3 lb per 94 lb cement about 3 volume cy
bottom to top by a piston pump
Grouting was terminated when grout appeared on top of hole withdrew casing in sections maintaining grout at top

Remarks
A 1 2 inch dia x 9 feet PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level
Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
Total of 10 bags of 94 lb cement were used to grout the borehole
Colloidal grout plant was used to mix grout
Meyco FIX Flowcable was added to mix grout about 3 lb per 94 lb cement about 3 volume cy
bottom to top by a piston pump
Grouting was terminated when grout appeared on top of hole withdrew casing in sections maintaining grout at top

Remarks
A 1 2 inch dia x 9 feet PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level
Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
Total of 11 bags of 94 lb cement were used to grout the borehole
Meyco FIX Flowcable was added to mix grout about 3 lb per 94 lb cement about 3 volume cy
bottom to top by a piston pump
Grouting was terminated when grout appeared on top of hole withdrew casing in sections maintaining grout at top

A 1 2 inch dia x 9 feet PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level

bottom to top by a piston pump

Remarks
A 1 2 inch dia x 9 feet PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level
Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
Total of 8 bags of 94 lb cement were used to grout the borehole
Meyco FIX Flowcable was added to mix grout about 3 lb per 94 lb cement about 3 volume cy
bottom to top by a piston pump
Grouting was terminated when grout appeared on top of hole withdrew casing in sections maintaining grout at top

Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
Total of 5 bags of 94 lb cement were used to grout the borehole
Colloidal grout plant was used to mix grout
Meyco FIX Flowcable was added to mix grout about 3 lb per 94 lb cement about 3 volume cy
bottom to top by a piston pump
Grouting was terminated when grout appeared on top of hole withdrew casing in sections maintaining grout at top

A 1 2 inch dia x 9 feet PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level
Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
Total of 6 bags of 94 lb cement were used to grout the borehole

bottom to top by a piston pump

Remarks
A 1 2 inch dia x 9 feet PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level
Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
Total of 5 bags of 94 lb cement were used to grout the borehole
Meyco FIX Flowcable was added to mix grout about 3 lb per 94 lb cement about 3 volume cy
bottom to top by a piston pump
Grouting was terminated when grout appeared on top of hole withdrew casing in sections maintaining grout at top

Colloidal grout plant was used to mix grout
Meyco FIX Flowcable was added to mix grout about 3 lb per 94 lb cement about 3 volume cy
bottom to top by a piston pump
Grouting was terminated when grout appeared on top of hole withdrew casing in sections maintaining grout at top

Remarks
A 1 2 inch dia x 9 feet PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level
Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
Total of 5 bags of 94 lb cement were used to grout the borehole
bottom to top by a piston pump
Grouting was terminated when grout appeared on top of hole withdrew casing in sections maintaining grout at top
Meyco FIX Flowcable was added to mix grout about 3 lb per 94 lb cement about 3 volume cy

A 1 2 inch dia x 9 feet PVC pipe was inserted into the grouted borehole to check the grout level
Grout was placed through a PVC tremie pipe and injected at lowest point of the hole progressively from
